NodePublishVolume\n41:    - util.MapBlockVolume\n42:    - ASW.MarkVolumeAsMounted\n43: \n44:  - operation_executor.UnmountVolume\n45:    - csi.GetPodDeviceMapPath\n46:    - util.UnmapBlockVolume\n47:    - csi.UnmapPodDevice\n48:      - NodeUnpublishVolume\n49:    - ASW.MarkVolumeAsUnmounted\n50: \n51:  - operation_executor.UnmountDevice\n52:    - csi.TearDownDevice\n53:      - NodeUnstageVolume\n54:    - ASW.MarkDeviceAsUnmounted\n55: \n56: After successful MountVolume for block volume, directory structure will be like below:\n57:   /dev/loopX ... Descriptor lock(Loopback device to mapFile under global map path)\n58:   /var/lib/kubelet/plugins/kubernetes.io/csi/volumeDevices/{specName}/dev/ ... Global map path\n59:   /var/lib/kubelet/plugins/kubernetes.io/csi/volumeDevices/{specName}/dev/{podUID} ... MapFile(Bind mount to publish Path)\n60:   /var/lib/kubelet/plugins/kubernetes.io/csi/volumeDevices/staging/{specName} ... Staging path\n61:   /var/lib/kubelet/plugins/kubernetes.io/csi/volumeDevices/publish/{specName}/{podUID} ... Publish path\n62:   /var/lib/kubelet/pods/{podUID}/volumeDevices/kubernetes.io~csi/ ... Pod device map path\n63:   /var/lib/kubelet/pods/{podUID}/volumeDevices/kubernetes.io~csi/{specName} ... MapFile(Symlink to publish path)\n64: */\n65: \n66: package csi\n67: \n68: import (\n69: \t\"context\"\n70: \t\"errors\"\n71: \t\"os\"\n72: \t\"path/filepath\"\n73: \n74: \tv1 \"k8s.io/api/core/v1\"\n75: \tstorage \"k8s.io/api/storage/v1\"\n76: \tmeta \"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/apis/meta/v1\"\n77: \t\"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/types\"\n78: \t\"k8s.io/client-go/kubernetes\"\n79: \t\"k8s.io/klog/v2\"\n80: \t\"k8s.io/kubernetes/pkg/util/removeall\"\n81: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes@7ae9c0d83a91bc9c7e35665665e662152fa39d13/-/blob/pkg/volume/csi/csi_block.go%3FL1-80"}}}

\"pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"PersistentVolumeController\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The CSI driver integration in kubernetes/kubernetes consists of multiple interconnected components that work together to enable Container Storage Interface (CSI) driver support:\\n\\n## CSI Node Plugin Client\\n\\nThe **CSI node plugin client** is implemented through:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go`: The main CSI plugin (csiPlugin struct) that serves as the volume plugin implementation. It manages CSI driver registration through the RegistrationHandler interface and coordinates with the volume plugin manager.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_client.go`: Defines the csiClient interface which abstracts all node-level CSI operations including NodeGetInfo, NodePublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeUnstageVolume, and NodeExpandVolume. This interface communicates with CSI drivers via gRPC.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_drivers_store.go`: Maintains a thread-safe store of registered CSI drivers with their endpoints and supported versions.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller\\n\\nThe **CSI volume attach/detach controller** implementation includes:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go`: The csiAttacher struct implements both the volume.Attacher and volume.Detacher interfaces. It handles volume attachment by creating VolumeAttachment objects and detachment by updating their status. The Attach and Detach methods orchestrate communication with CSI drivers through gRPC.\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go`: The main attach/detach controller that manages the lifecycle of volume attachments. It maintains desired and actual state of world, uses the attacherDetacher OperationExecutor to perform operations, and integrates with CSI through CSINodeLister for topology-aware scheduling.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Provisioner\\n\\nThe **CSI volume provisioner** is integrated into:\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go`: The PersistentVolumeController handles dynamic provisioning by creating external provisioner requests and includes support for CSI migration from in-tree plugins. The provisionClaimOperationExternal method routes provisioning requests to the appropriate CSI driver based on StorageClass configuration.\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller_base.go`: Provides the base controller setup, initializes the CSI translator for in-tree plugin migration, and manages the CSI migration manager.\\n\\n## CSI Node Integration\\n\\nThe CSI node integration for volume operations includes:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_mounter.go`: The csiMountMgr struct implements mount/unmount operations. SetUpAt performs node staging and publishing, while TearDownAt handles unpublishing and unstaging of volumes.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_block.go`: The csiBlockMapper handles block device operations through SetUpDevice (NodeStageVolume) and TearDownDevice (NodeUnstageVolume), managing device staging and publishing for block volumes.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go`: The nodeInfoManager maintains CSI node information including driver node IDs, topology keys, and allocatable resources. The UpdateCSIDriver method updates the CSINode object with driver-specific information.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_node_updater.go`: The csiNodeUpdater watches CSIDriver objects and manages per-driver goroutines that periodically update CSINodeDriver allocatable information.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Expansion\\n\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/expander.go`: Implements NodeExpand for online volume expansion by querying driver capabilities and calling the CSI NodeExpandVolume RPC.\\n\\n## Supporting Utilities\\n\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_util.go`: Provides utility functions for credential management, volume data persistence, and secret handling.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_metrics.go`: Implements the MetricsProvider interface for reporting volume metrics like capacity and usage.\\n\\n## Integration Flow\\n\\nThe CSI driver integration works as follows: When a CSI driver registers, the RegistrationHandler validates it and stores it in DriversStore. For volume operations, the attach/detach controller uses the csiAttacher to create VolumeAttachment objects, triggering external-attacher components. The PersistentVolumeController orchestrates provisioning by identifying CSI-based StorageClasses and creating provision requests. of multiple interconnected components that work together to enable Container Storage Interface (CSI) driver support:\\n\\n## CSI Node Plugin Client\\n\\nThe **CSI node plugin client** is implemented through:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go`: The main CSI plugin (csiPlugin struct) that serves as the volume plugin implementation. It manages CSI driver registration through the RegistrationHandler interface and coordinates with the volume plugin manager.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_client.go`: Defines the csiClient interface which abstracts all node-level CSI operations including NodeGetInfo, NodePublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeUnstageVolume, and NodeExpandVolume. This interface communicates with CSI drivers via gRPC.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_drivers_store.go`: Maintains a thread-safe store of registered CSI drivers with their endpoints and supported versions.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller\\n\\nThe **CSI volume attach/detach controller** implementation includes:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go`: The csiAttacher struct implements both the volume.Attacher and volume.Detacher interfaces. It handles volume attachment by creating VolumeAttachment objects and detachment by updating their status. The Attach and Detach methods orchestrate communication with CSI drivers through gRPC.\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go`: The main attach/detach controller that manages the lifecycle of volume attachments. It maintains desired and actual state of world, uses the attacherDetacher OperationExecutor to perform operations, and integrates with CSI through CSINodeLister for topology-aware scheduling.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Provisioner\\n\\nThe **CSI volume provisioner** is integrated into:\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go`: The PersistentVolumeController handles dynamic provisioning by creating external provisioner requests and includes support for CSI migration from in-tree plugins. The provisionClaimOperationExternal method routes provisioning requests to the appropriate CSI driver based on StorageClass configuration.\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller_base.go`: Provides the base controller setup, initializes the CSI translator for in-tree plugin migration, and manages the CSI migration manager.\\n\\n## CSI Node Integration\\n\\nThe CSI node integration for volume operations includes:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_mounter.go`: The csiMountMgr struct implements mount/unmount operations. SetUpAt performs node staging and publishing, while TearDownAt handles unpublishing and unstaging of volumes.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_block.go`: The csiBlockMapper handles block device operations through SetUpDevice (NodeStageVolume) and TearDownDevice (NodeUnstageVolume), managing device staging and publishing for block volumes.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go`: The nodeInfoManager maintains CSI node information including driver node IDs, topology keys, and allocatable resources. The UpdateCSIDriver method updates the CSINode object with driver-specific information.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_node_updater.go`: The csiNodeUpdater watches CSIDriver objects and manages per-driver goroutines that periodically update CSINodeDriver allocatable information.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Expansion\\n\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/expander.go`: Implements NodeExpand for online volume expansion by querying driver capabilities and calling the CSI NodeExpandVolume RPC.\\n\\n## Supporting Utilities\\n\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_util.go`: Provides utility functions for credential management, volume data persistence, and secret handling.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_metrics.go`: Implements the MetricsProvider interface for reporting volume metrics like capacity and usage.\\n\\n## Integration Flow\\n\\nThe CSI driver integration works as follows: When a CSI driver registers, the RegistrationHandler validates it and stores it in DriversStore. For volume operations, the attach/detach controller uses the csiAttacher to create VolumeAttachment objects, triggering external-attacher components. The PersistentVolumeController orchestrates provisioning by identifying CSI-based StorageClasses and creating provision requests. On nodes, the csiMountMgr and csiBlockMapper implement mount/unmount and device setup operations using the csiClient. Node information is managed by nodeInfoManager which updates CSINode objects with topology and capacity information.
